NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
N.C. Naveen Kumar, a Male child, born to Thiru N. Chandrasekaran, on 18th May 1995, residing at
No. 3/376, Padaiyachi Street, Kottapalayam, Thuraiyur, Thiruchirappalli-621 003, has been living as a Transgender women.
I have been granted Identity Card No. TRY/066/2020, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and 
N.M.P. Department. By this, I may be treated as Transgender woman and shall henceforth be known as C. NIVINYA SREE
Thiruchirappalli, 
N.C. NAVEEN KUMAR
2nd August 2021.
